<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<h3 id="default-value" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#default-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Default Value</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultValue</code> prop to specify which item should be expanded by default.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> props to control the expanded items.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the accordion is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useAccordion</code> hook. This way
you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="collapsible" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#collapsible"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Collapsible</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">collapsible</code> prop to allow the user to collapse all panels.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="multiple" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#multiple"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Multiple</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">multiple</code> prop to allow multiple panels to be expanded simultaneously.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="horizontal" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#horizontal"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Horizontal</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, the Accordion is oriented vertically. Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">orientation</code> prop to switch to a horizontal layout.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="lazy-mount" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#lazy-mount"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Lazy Mount</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">lazyMount</code> prop to defer rendering of accordion content until the item is expanded. Combine with
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">unmountOnExit</code> to unmount content when collapsed, freeing up resources.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Accordion.Context</code> or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useAccordionContext</code> to access the accordion state.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="item-state" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#item-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Item State</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Accordion.ItemContext</code> or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useAccordionItemContext</code> to access the state of an accordion item.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="content-animation" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#content-animation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Content Animation</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--height</code> and/or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--width</code> CSS variables to animate the size of the content when it expands or closes:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">@keyframes</span><span style="color:#FFA657"> slideDown</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  from</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    opacity</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0.01</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  to</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    opacity</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">@keyframes</span><span style="color:#FFA657"> slideUp</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  from</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    opacity</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  to</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    opacity</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0.01</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">    height</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;accordion&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;item-content&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-state</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;open&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  animation</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: slideDown </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">250</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">ms</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> ease-in-out</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;accordion&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;item-content&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-state</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;closed&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>

<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

<h3 id="context-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This component complies with the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/accordion/" class="link">Accordion WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"accordion\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cAccordion.Root\u003e\n  \u003cAccordion.Item\u003e\n    \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator /\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cAccordion.ItemContent /\u003e\n  \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n\u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### Default Value\n\nSet the `defaultValue` prop to specify which item should be expanded by default.\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/react/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']}\u003e\n      {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n        \u003cAccordion.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} value={item.value}\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger className={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n            {item.title}\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemContent className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/solid/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']}\u003e\n      \u003cIndex each={items}\u003e\n        {(item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item().value}\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n              {item().title}\n              \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item().content}\u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/vue/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cAccordion.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :defaultValue=\"['ark-ui']\"\u003e\n    \u003cAccordion.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :value=\"item.value\"\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger :class=\"styles.ItemTrigger\"\u003e\n        {{ item.title }}\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent :class=\"styles.ItemContent\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemBody\"\u003e{{ item.content }}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/svelte/accordion'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    {\n      value: 'ark-ui',\n      title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n      content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'getting-started',\n      title: 'How to get started?',\n      content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'maintainers',\n      title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n      content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n    },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']}\u003e\n  {#each items as item (item.value)}\n    \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item.value}\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n        {item.title}\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  {/each}\n\u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nUse the `value` and `onValueChange` props to control the expanded items.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/react/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = useState\u003cstring[]\u003e([])\n\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root className={styles.Root} value={value} onValueChange={(details) =\u003e setValue(details.value)}\u003e\n      {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n        \u003cAccordion.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} value={item.value}\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger className={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n            {item.title}\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemContent className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/solid/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = createSignal\u003cstring[]\u003e([])\n\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} value={value()} onValueChange={(details) =\u003e setValue(details.value)}\u003e\n      \u003cIndex each={items}\u003e\n        {(item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item().value}\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n              {item().title}\n              \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item().content}\u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/vue/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nconst value = ref\u003cstring[]\u003e([])\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cAccordion.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model=\"value\"\u003e\n    \u003cAccordion.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :value=\"item.value\"\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger :class=\"styles.ItemTrigger\"\u003e\n        {{ item.title }}\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent :class=\"styles.ItemContent\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemBody\"\u003e{{ item.content }}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/svelte/accordion'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\n  let value = $state\u003cstring[]\u003e([])\n\n  const items = [\n    {\n      value: 'ark-ui',\n      title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n      content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'getting-started',\n      title: 'How to get started?',\n      content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'maintainers',\n      title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n      content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n    },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} bind:value\u003e\n  {#each items as item (item.value)}\n    \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item.value}\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n        {item.title}\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  {/each}\n\u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the accordion is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useAccordion` hook. This way\nyou can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion, useAccordion } from '@ark-ui/react/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const accordion = useAccordion({\n    multiple: true,\n    defaultValue: ['ark-ui'],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eValue: {JSON.stringify(accordion.value)}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n      \u003cAccordion.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={accordion}\u003e\n        {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cAccordion.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} value={item.value}\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger className={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n              {item.title}\n              \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemContent className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Accordion.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion, useAccordion } from '@ark-ui/solid/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const accordion = useAccordion({\n    multiple: true,\n    defaultValue: ['ark-ui'],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eValue: {JSON.stringify(accordion().value)}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n      \u003cAccordion.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={accordion}\u003e\n        \u003cIndex each={items}\u003e\n          {(item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item().value}\u003e\n              \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n                {item().title}\n                \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                  \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n              \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item().content}\u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/Index\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Accordion, useAccordion } from '@ark-ui/vue/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\nconst accordion = useAccordion({\n  multiple: true,\n  defaultValue: ['ark-ui'],\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv  \u003cAccordion.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :value=\"item.value\"\u003e\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger :class=\"styles.ItemTrigger\"\u003e\n          {{ item.title }}\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n            \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemContent :class=\"styles.ItemContent\"\u003e\n          \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemBody\"\u003e{{ item.content }}\u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Accordion, useAccordion } from '@ark-ui/svelte/accordion'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const accordion = useAccordion({\n    id,\n    defaultValue: ['ark-ui'],\n  })\n\n  const items = [\n    {\n      value: 'ark-ui',\n      title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n      content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'getting-started',\n      title: 'How to get started?',\n      content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'maintainers',\n      title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n      content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n    },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003eValue: {JSON.stringify(accordion().value)}\u003c/output\u003e\n \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n          {item.title}\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n            \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Accordion.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Collapsible\n\nUse the `collapsible` prop to allow the user to collapse all panels.\n\n**Example: collapsible**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/react/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Collapsible = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']} collapsible\u003e\n      {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n        \u003cAccordion.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} value={item.value}\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger className={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n            {item.title}\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemContent className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/solid/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Collapsible = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']} collapsible\u003e\n      \u003cIndex  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/vue/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cAccordion.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :defaultValue=\"['ark-ui']\" collapsible\u003e\n    \u003cAccordion.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :value=\"item.value\"\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger :class=\"styles.ItemTrigger\"\u003e\n        {{ item.title }}\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent :class=\"styles.ItemContent\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemBody\"\u003e{{ item.content }}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/svelte/accordion'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    {\n      value: 'ark-ui',\n      title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n      content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'getting-started',\n      title: 'How to get started?',\n      content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'maintainers',\n      title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n      content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n    },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']} collapsible\u003e\n  {#each items as item (item.value)}\n    \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item.value}\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n        {item.title}\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  {/each}\n\u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Multiple\n\nUse the `multiple` prop to allow multiple panels to be expanded simultaneously.\n\n**Example: multiple**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/react/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Multiple = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']} multiple\u003e\n      {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n        \u003cAccordion.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} value={item.value}\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger className={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n            {item.title}\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemContent className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/solid/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Multiple = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']} multiple\u003e\n      \u003cIndex each={items}\u003e\n        {(item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item().value}\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n              {item().title}\n              \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item().content}\u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/vue/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cAccordion.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :defaultValue=\"['ark-ui']\" multiple\u003e\n    \u003cAccordion.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :value=\"item.value\"\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger :class=\"styles.ItemTrigger\"\u003e\n        {{ item.title }}\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent :class=\"styles.ItemContent\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.ItemBody\"\u003e{{ item.content }}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/svelte/accordion'\n  import { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    {\n      value: 'ark-ui',\n      title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n      content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'getting-started',\n      title: 'How to get started?',\n      content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'maintainers',\n      title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n      content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n    },\n value={item.value}\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n        {item.title}\n        \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n          \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  {/each}\n\u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Horizontal\n\nBy default, the Accordion is oriented vertically. Use the `orientation` prop to switch to a horizontal layout.\n\n**Example: horizontal**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/react/accordion'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Horizontal = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']} orientation=\"horizontal\"\u003e\n      {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n        \u003cAccordion.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} value={item.value}\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger className={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e{item.title}\u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemContent className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={`${styles.ItemBody} ${styles.Centered}`}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/solid/accordion'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const Horizontal = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']} orientation=\"horizontal\"\u003e\n      \u003cIndex each={items}\u003e\n        {(item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item().value}\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e{item().title}\u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={`${styles.ItemBody} ${styles.Centered}`}\u003e{item().content}\u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/vue/accordion'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cAccordion.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :defaultValue=\"['ark-ui']\" orientation=\"horizontal\"\u003e\n    \u003cAccordion.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item.value\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :value=\"item.value\"\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger :class=\"styles.ItemTrigger\"\u003e{{ item.title }}\u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent :class=\"styles.ItemContent\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"[styles.ItemBody, styles.Centered]\"\u003e{{ item.content }}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/svelte/accordion'\n  import styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    {\n      value: 'ark-ui',\n      title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n      content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'getting-started',\n      title: 'How to get started?',\n      content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'maintainers',\n      title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n      content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n    },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={['ark-ui']} orientation=\"horizontal\"\u003e\n  {#each items as item (item.value)}\n    \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item.value}\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e{item.title}\u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={`${styles.ItemBody} ${styles.Centered}`}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n  {/each}\n\u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Lazy Mount\n\nUse the `lazyMount` prop to defer rendering of accordion content until the item is expanded. Combine with\n`unmountOnExit` to unmount content when collapsed, freeing up resources.\n\n**Example: lazy-mount**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/react/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const LazyMount = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root className={styles.Root} lazyMount unmountOnExit\u003e\n      {items.map((item) =\u003e (\n        \u003cAccordion.Item className={styles.Item} key={item.value} value={item.value}\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger className={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n            {item.title}\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator className={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n              \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cAccordion.ItemContent className={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item.content}\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n        \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/solid/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nexport const LazyMount = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cAccordion.Root class={styles.Root} lazyMount unmountOnExit\u003e\n      \u003cIndex each={items}\u003e\n        {(item) =\u003e (\n          \u003cAccordion.Item class={styles.Item} value={item().value}\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemTrigger class={styles.ItemTrigger}\u003e\n              {item().title}\n              \u003cAccordion.ItemIndicator class={styles.ItemIndicator}\u003e\n                \u003cChevronDownIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Accordion.ItemIndicator\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cAccordion.ItemContent class={styles.ItemContent}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.ItemBody}\u003e{item().content}\u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/Accordion.ItemContent\u003e\n          \u003c/Accordion.Item\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/Index\u003e\n    \u003c/Accordion.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n    content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n  },\n]\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Accordion } from '@ark-ui/vue/accordion'\nimport { ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  {\n    value: 'ark-ui',\n    title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n    content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'getting-started',\n    title: 'How to get started?',\n    content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'maintainers',\n    title: 'Who maintains ChevronDownIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/accordion.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    {\n      value: 'ark-ui',\n      title: 'What is Ark UI?',\n      content: 'A headless component library for building accessible web apps.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'getting-started',\n      title: 'How to get started?',\n      content: 'Install the package and import the components you need.',\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'maintainers',\n      title: 'Who maintains this project?',\n      content: 'Ark UI is maintained by the Chakra UI team.',\n    },\n
